# Patch Notes

## Summary
- Uniques: 10 added, 3 removed, 1234 modified
- Sets: 0 added, 0 removed, 2 modified
- Runewords: 11 added, 0 removed, 50 modified
- Base Items: 0 added, 0 removed, 0 modified
- Cube Recipes: 0 added, 0 removed, 0 modified
